import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

# Text-based autofill (your old one)
from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

# Azure OCR autofill (we add this now)
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    """
    Uses Azure Document Intelligence prebuilt-invoice model.
    Returns a dict with fields we care about.
    """
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        # Azure returns "content" as the raw seen text
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        # Sometimes valueCurrency exists, sometimes it's just content text
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    # invoice date parsing (Azure often gives YYYY-MM-DD)
    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),       # best match for "Total HT"
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),  # extra (not used in XML yet)
    }


st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Converter (Local Demo)")

uploaded_pdf = st.file_uploader("Upload your invoice PDF", type=["pdf"])

# -------------------------
# Session defaults
# -------------------------
if "invoice_number" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.invoice_number = "INV-001"
if "invoice_date" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.invoice_date = date.today()
if "seller_name" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_name = "My Company"
if "seller_siret" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_siret = "12345678900011"
if "seller_vat" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_vat = "FR11123456789"
if "buyer_name" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.buyer_name = "Customer Name"
if "total_ht_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.total_ht_str = "100.00"
if "vat_rate_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.vat_rate_str = "20"

# -------------------------
# Auto-fill buttons
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf is not None:
    col1, col2 = st.columns(2)

    with col1:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)"):
            pdf_bytes_for_autofill = uploaded_pdf.read()
            fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_for_autofill)

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Re-check fields below.")

    with col2:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)"):
            uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
            pdf_bytes_for_ocr = uploaded_pdf.read()

            try:
                fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_for_ocr)
            except Exception as e:
                st.error("❌ Azure OCR failed. Check your .env keys or Azure resource.")
                st.code(str(e))
                st.stop()

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Re-check fields below.")

# -------------------------
# Form inputs
# -------------------------
st.subheader("Invoice details")
invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number", key="invoice_number")
invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date", key="invoice_date")

st.subheader("Seller (your company)")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", key="seller_name")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", key="seller_siret")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", key="seller_vat")

st.subheader("Buyer (your customer)")
buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name", key="buyer_name")

st.subheader("Amounts")
total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)", key="total_ht_str")
vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)", key="vat_rate_str")

# -------------------------
# Generate
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        # Validate XML before embedding
        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        # Re-read PDF bytes
        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        st.success("✅ Done! Download your Factur-X PDF below:")
        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
        )
else:
    st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

# Text-based autofill
from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

# Azure OCR autofill
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    """
    Uses Azure Document Intelligence prebuilt-invoice model.
    Returns a dict with fields we care about.
    """
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }


st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Converter (Local Demo)")

uploaded_pdf = st.file_uploader("Upload your invoice PDF", type=["pdf"])

# -------------------------
# Session defaults
# -------------------------
if "invoice_number" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.invoice_number = "INV-001"
if "invoice_date" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.invoice_date = date.today()
if "seller_name" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_name = "My Company"
if "seller_siret" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_siret = "12345678900011"
if "seller_vat" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_vat = "FR11123456789"
if "buyer_name" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.buyer_name = "Customer Name"
if "total_ht_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.total_ht_str = "100.00"
if "vat_rate_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.vat_rate_str = "20"

# -------------------------
# Auto-fill buttons
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf is not None:
    col1, col2 = st.columns(2)

    with col1:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)"):
            pdf_bytes_for_autofill = uploaded_pdf.read()
            fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_for_autofill)

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Re-check fields below.")

    with col2:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)"):
            uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
            pdf_bytes_for_ocr = uploaded_pdf.read()

            try:
                fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_for_ocr)
            except Exception as e:
                st.error("❌ Azure OCR failed. Check your .env keys or Azure resource.")
                st.code(str(e))
                st.stop()

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Re-check fields below.")

# -------------------------
# Form inputs
# -------------------------
st.subheader("Invoice details")
invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number", key="invoice_number")
invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date", key="invoice_date")

st.subheader("Seller (your company)")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", key="seller_name")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", key="seller_siret")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", key="seller_vat")

st.subheader("Buyer (your customer)")
buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name", key="buyer_name")

st.subheader("Amounts")
total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)", key="total_ht_str")
vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)", key="vat_rate_str")

# -------------------------
# Generate
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        # Validate XML before embedding
        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        # ✅ NEW: Download XML button (debug / proof)
        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
        )

        # Re-read PDF bytes
        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        st.success("✅ Done! Download your Factur-X PDF below:")
        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
        )
else:
    st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

# Text-based autofill
from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

# Azure OCR autofill
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }

    st.session_state.buyer_name = "Customer Name"

    st.session_state.total_ht_str = "100.00"
if "vat_rate_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.vat_rate_str = "20"

# -------------------------
# Auto-fill buttons

if uploaded_pdf is not None:
    col1, col2 = st.columns(2)

    with col1:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)"):
            pdf_bytes_for_autofill = uploaded_pdf.read()
            fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_for_autofill)

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Re-check fields below.")

    with col2:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)"):
            if not use_azure:
                st.warning("Azure OCR is OFF. Turn on the checkbox above to use it.")
                st.stop()

            uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
            pdf_bytes_for_ocr = uploaded_pdf.read()

            try:
                fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_for_ocr)
            except Exception as e:
                st.error("❌ Azure OCR failed. Check your .env keys or Azure resource.")
                st.code(str(e))
                st.stop()

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Re-check fields below.")

# -------------------------
# Form inputs
# -------------------------
st.subheader("Invoice details")
invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number", key="invoice_number")
invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date", key="invoice_date")

st.subheader("Seller (your company)")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", key="seller_name")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", key="seller_siret")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", key="seller_vat")

st.subheader("Buyer (your customer)")
buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name", key="buyer_name")

st.subheader("Amounts")
total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)", key="total_ht_str")
vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)", key="vat_rate_str")

# -------------------------
# Generate
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
        )

        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        st.success("✅ Done! Download your Factur-X PDF below:")
        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
        )
else:
    st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")

Next step (only 1 step): Make the app save the generated PDF into your output/ folder automatically

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation
from pathlib import Path

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }

if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:

            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        # Create output folder + save XML locally
        out_dir = Path("output")
        out_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        xml_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml"
        xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)

        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
        )
        st.info(f"📁 Saved XML locally to: {xml_path}")

        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        # Save PDF locally
        pdf_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf"
        pdf_path.write_bytes(out_bytes)

        st.success("✅ Done! Download your Factur-X PDF below:")
        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
        )
        st.info(f"📁 Saved PDF locally to: {pdf_path}")
else:
    st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }

st.title("Factur-X Converter (Local Demo)")
st.caption("Tip: OCR calls a cloud service. Use it only when needed.")

use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (may cost money later)", value=True)

uploaded_pdf = st.file_uploader("Upload your invoice PDF", type=["pdf"])

# -------------------------
# Session defaults
# -------------------------
if "invoice_number" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.invoice_number = "INV-001"
if "invoice_date" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.invoice_date = date.today()
if "seller_name" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_name = "My Company"
if "seller_siret" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_siret = "12345678900011"
if "seller_vat" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.seller_vat = "FR11123456789"
if "buyer_name" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.buyer_name = "Customer Name"
if "total_ht_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.total_ht_str = "100.00"
if "vat_rate_str" not in st.session_state:
    st.session_state.vat_rate_str = "20"

# -------------------------
# Auto-fill buttons
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf is not None:
    col1, col2 = st.columns(2)

    with col1:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)"):
            pdf_bytes_for_autofill = uploaded_pdf.read()
            fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_for_autofill)

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Re-check fields below.")

    with col2:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)"):
            if not use_azure:
                st.warning("Azure OCR is OFF. Turn on the checkbox above to use it.")
                st.stop()

            uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
            pdf_bytes_for_ocr = uploaded_pdf.read()

            try:
                fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_for_ocr)
            except Exception as e:
                st.error("❌ Azure OCR failed. Check your .env keys or Azure resource.")
                st.code(str(e))
                st.stop()

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Re-check fields below.")

# -------------------------
# Form inputs
# -------------------------
st.subheader("Invoice details")
invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number", key="invoice_number")
invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date", key="invoice_date")

st.subheader("Seller (your company)")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", key="seller_name")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", key="seller_siret")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", key="seller_vat")

st.subheader("Buyer (your customer)")
buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name", key="buyer_name")

st.subheader("Amounts")
total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)", key="total_ht_str")
vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)", key="vat_rate_str")

# -------------------------
# Show calculated amounts (read-only)
# -------------------------
try:
    total_ht_preview = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
    vat_rate_preview = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
    vat_amount_preview = (total_ht_preview * vat_rate_preview / Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    total_ttc_preview = (total_ht_preview + vat_amount_preview).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)

    st.caption(f"📌 VAT amount: {vat_amount_preview}  |  Total TTC: {total_ttc_preview}")
except Exception:
    st.caption("📌 VAT amount: (enter valid numbers)  |  Total TTC: (enter valid numbers)")

# -------------------------
# Generate
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        out_dir = Path("output")
        out_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        xml_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml"
        xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)

        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
        )
        st.info(f"📁 Saved XML locally to: {xml_path}")

        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        pdf_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf"
        pdf_path.write_bytes(out_bytes)

        st.success("✅ Done! Download your Factur-X PDF below:")
        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
        )
        st.info(f"📁 Saved PDF locally to: {pdf_path}")
else:
    st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")

Next step (only 1 step): Make OCR also fill the VAT rate automatically
Right now Azure gives us:

SubTotal (HT) ✅

InvoiceTotal (TTC) ✅

So we can calculate VAT rate automatically like a smart calculator:

VAT rate % = (TTC − HT) / HT × 100

That means the user won’t type VAT rate anymore (most of the time).

✅ We will do ONE simple change: update the Azure OCR function to set vat_rate_str.

✅ Replace your app.py with this FULL code (copy/paste)
This is your same file, only Azure part is smarter.

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    total_ht_str = number("SubTotal")
    total_ttc_str = number("InvoiceTotal")

    # ✅ Calculate VAT rate if we have both HT and TTC
    vat_rate_str = None
    try:
        if total_ht_str and total_ttc_str:
            ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            ttc = Decimal(str(total_ttc_str).replace(",", "."))
            if ht > 0 and ttc >= ht:
                vat_amount = ttc - ht
                vat_rate = (vat_amount / ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
                vat_rate_str = str(vat_rate)
    except Exception:
        vat_rate_str = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": total_ht_str,
        "vat_rate_str": vat_rate_str,     # ✅ NEW autofill
        "total_ttc_str": total_ttc_str,
    }

    vat_amount_preview = (total_ht_preview * vat_rate_preview / Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    total_ttc_preview = (total_ht_preview + vat_amount_preview).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    st.caption(f"📌 VAT amount: {vat_amount_preview}  |  Total TTC: {total_ttc_preview}")

            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,

            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,

Next step (only 1 step): Make it “France-ready” by adding Buyer VAT + Buyer SIRET fields
Right now you only collect:

Seller VAT + Seller SIRET ✅
But for French B2B invoices, you usually need Buyer identifiers too (at least VAT, sometimes SIRET).

So we’ll add 2 new inputs:
✅ Buyer SIRET
✅ Buyer VAT

Even if OCR can’t always read them, the user can type them.

✅ Full app.py (copy/paste)
This is your current working version + adds buyer_siret and buyer_vat inputs + passes them into XML builder only if your XML builder supports them.

⚠️ Important: if your build_facturx_minimum_xml() doesn’t accept buyer fields yet, we won’t crash — we’ll safely ignore them.

Copy/paste entire file:

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    total_ht_str = number("SubTotal")
    total_ttc_str = number("InvoiceTotal")

    vat_rate_str = None
    try:
        if total_ht_str and total_ttc_str:
            ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            ttc = Decimal(str(total_ttc_str).replace(",", "."))
            if ht > 0 and ttc >= ht:
                vat_amount = ttc - ht
                vat_rate = (vat_amount / ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
                vat_rate_str = str(vat_rate)
    except Exception:
        vat_rate_str = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": total_ht_str,
        "vat_rate_str": vat_rate_str,
        "total_ttc_str": total_ttc_str,
    }


st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Converter (Local Demo)")
st.caption("Tip: OCR calls a cloud service. Use it only when needed.")

use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (may cost money later)", value=True)

uploaded_pdf = st.file_uploader("Upload your invoice PDF", type=["pdf"])

defaults = {
    "invoice_number": "INV-001",
    "invoice_date": date.today(),
    "seller_name": "My Company",
    "seller_siret": "12345678900011",
    "seller_vat": "FR11123456789",
    "buyer_name": "Customer Name",
    "buyer_siret": "",
    "buyer_vat": "",
    "total_ht_str": "100.00",
    "vat_rate_str": "20",
}
for k, v in defaults.items():
    if k not in st.session_state:
        st.session_state[k] = v

# -------------------------
# Auto-fill buttons

if uploaded_pdf is not None:
    col1, col2 = st.columns(2)

    with col1:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)"):
            pdf_bytes_for_autofill = uploaded_pdf.read()
            fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_for_autofill)

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Re-check fields below.")

    with col2:
        if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)"):
            if not use_azure:
                st.warning("Azure OCR is OFF. Turn on the checkbox above to use it.")
                st.stop()

            uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
            pdf_bytes_for_ocr = uploaded_pdf.read()

            try:
                fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_for_ocr)
            except Exception as e:
                st.error("❌ Azure OCR failed. Check your .env keys or Azure resource.")
                st.code(str(e))
                st.stop()

            for k, v in fields.items():
                if v is None:
                    continue
                st.session_state[k] = v

            st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Re-check fields below.")

# -------------------------
# Form inputs
# -------------------------
st.subheader("Invoice details")
invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number", key="invoice_number")
invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date", key="invoice_date")

st.subheader("Seller (your company)")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", key="seller_name")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", key="seller_siret")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", key="seller_vat")

st.subheader("Buyer (your customer)")
buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name", key="buyer_name")
buyer_siret = st.text_input("Buyer SIRET (optional)", key="buyer_siret")
buyer_vat = st.text_input("Buyer VAT (optional)", key="buyer_vat")

st.subheader("Amounts")
total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)", key="total_ht_str")
vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)", key="vat_rate_str")

# Preview totals
try:
    total_ht_preview = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
    vat_rate_preview = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
    vat_amount_preview = (total_ht_preview * vat_rate_preview / Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    total_ttc_preview = (total_ht_preview + vat_amount_preview).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    st.caption(f"📌 VAT amount: {vat_amount_preview}  |  Total TTC: {total_ttc_preview}")
except Exception:
    st.caption("📌 VAT amount: (enter valid numbers)  |  Total TTC: (enter valid numbers)")

# -------------------------
# Generate
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        # Build args dictionary so we can safely add optional fields
        build_args = dict(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        # Add optional buyer identifiers (only if user filled them)
        if buyer_siret.strip():
            build_args["buyer_siret"] = buyer_siret.strip()
        if buyer_vat.strip():
            build_args["buyer_vat"] = buyer_vat.strip()

        # Call builder (if builder doesn't support buyer_* yet, ignore gracefully)
        try:
            xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(**build_args)
        except TypeError:
            # fallback without buyer fields
            build_args.pop("buyer_siret", None)
            build_args.pop("buyer_vat", None)
            xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(**build_args)

        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        out_dir = Path("output")
        out_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        xml_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml"
        xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
        )
        st.info(f"📁 Saved XML locally to: {xml_path}")

        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        pdf_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf"
        pdf_path.write_bytes(out_bytes)

        st.success("✅ Done! Download your Factur-X PDF below:")
        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
        )
        st.info(f"📁 Saved PDF locally to: {pdf_path}")
else:
    st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import io
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    total_ht_str = number("SubTotal")
    total_ttc_str = number("InvoiceTotal")

    vat_rate_str = None
    try:
        if total_ht_str and total_ttc_str:
            ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            ttc = Decimal(str(total_ttc_str).replace(",", "."))
            if ht > 0 and ttc >= ht:
                vat_amount = ttc - ht
                vat_rate = (vat_amount / ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
                vat_rate_str = str(vat_rate)
    except Exception:
        vat_rate_str = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": total_ht_str,
        "vat_rate_str": vat_rate_str,
        "total_ttc_str": total_ttc_str,
    }

    total_ttc_preview = (total_ht_preview + vat_amount_preview).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)

    st.caption("📌 VAT amount: (enter valid numbers)  |  Total TTC: (enter valid numbers)")

# -------------------------
# Generate
# -------------------------
if uploaded_pdf:
    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(str(total_ht_str).replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(str(vat_rate_str).replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        build_args = dict(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,

        )

        if buyer_siret.strip():

        if buyer_vat.strip():

            build_args.pop("buyer_siret", None)

        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
            xml_valid = True
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        out_dir = Path("output")
        out_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        xml_path = out_dir / f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml"
        xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)

        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{invoice_number}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
        )

        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path
import io
import os
import re
import zipfile

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text


# -------------------------
# Helpers
# -------------------------
def safe_name(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return "invoice"
    s = re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+", "_", s)
    return s[:80]


def to_decimal(s: str):
    if s is None:
        return None
    try:
        return Decimal(str(s).replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None


def compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht: Decimal, total_ttc: Decimal):
    if total_ht is None or total_ttc is None:
        return None
    if total_ht <= 0 or total_ttc < total_ht:
        return None
    vat_amount = total_ttc - total_ht
    rate = (vat_amount / total_ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    return rate


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }


# -------------------------
# UI
# -------------------------
st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Bulk Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Bulk Converter (Local Demo)")
st.caption("Bulk mode: upload many PDFs → download one ZIP with PDFs + XML + reports.")

use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (best results, may cost money later)", value=True)

st.subheader("Seller (your company) — typed once for all PDFs")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", value="My Company")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", value="12345678900011")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", value="FR11123456789")

st.subheader("Defaults (used if OCR misses something)")
default_buyer_name = st.text_input("Default Buyer Name", value="Customer")
default_vat_rate = st.text_input("Default VAT rate % (used only if we cannot compute)", value="20")

uploaded_pdfs = st.file_uploader(
    "Upload invoice PDFs (you can select many)",
    type=["pdf"],
    accept_multiple_files=True
)

st.divider()

if not uploaded_pdfs:
    st.info("Upload PDFs to enable bulk conversion.")
    st.stop()

st.write(f"📄 PDFs selected: **{len(uploaded_pdfs)}**")

if st.button("Convert ALL to Factur-X (ZIP)"):
    out_root = Path("output")
    out_root.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    batch_folder = out_root / f"bulk_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
    batch_folder.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

    results = []
    zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()

    progress = st.progress(0)
    status = st.empty()

    # Pre-parse default VAT rate
    default_vat_rate_dec = to_decimal(default_vat_rate)

    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
        for i, up in enumerate(uploaded_pdfs, start=1):
            status.write(f"⏳ Processing {i}/{len(uploaded_pdfs)}: **{up.name}**")
            progress.progress(int((i - 1) / len(uploaded_pdfs) * 100))

            try:
                pdf_bytes = up.read()

                # 1) Extract fields
                if use_azure:
                    fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes)
                    ocr_used = "azure"
                else:
                    fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes)
                    ocr_used = "text"

                # 2) Build per-invoice values (with fallbacks)
                inv_no = fields.get("invoice_number") or Path(up.name).stem
                inv_no = safe_name(inv_no)

                inv_date = fields.get("invoice_date") or date.today()
                buyer_name = (fields.get("buyer_name") or default_buyer_name or "Customer").strip()

                total_ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                total_ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))

                # VAT rate: compute from HT/TTC if possible, else fallback to default
                vat_rate = None
                if total_ht is not None and total_ttc is not None:
                    vat_rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht, total_ttc)

                if vat_rate is None:
                    vat_rate = default_vat_rate_dec

                # Hard requirements for our MINIMUM XML builder:
                if total_ht is None:
                    raise Exception("Missing Total HT (SubTotal). OCR could not find it.")
                if vat_rate is None:
                    raise Exception("Missing VAT rate. OCR could not compute it and default VAT rate is invalid.")

                # 3) Build XML
                build_args = dict(
                    invoice_number=inv_no,
                    invoice_date=inv_date,
                    seller_name=seller_name,
                    seller_siret=seller_siret,
                    seller_vat=seller_vat,
                    buyer_name=buyer_name,
                    total_ht=total_ht,
                    vat_rate_percent=vat_rate,
                )

                xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(**build_args)

                # 4) Validate XML
                validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)

                # 5) Embed into PDF
                out_pdf_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

                # 6) Save locally
                xml_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml"
                pdf_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf"
                report_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_report.txt"

                xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
                pdf_path.write_bytes(out_pdf_bytes)

                report_text = f"""FACTUR-X BULK REPORT
-------------------
SourceFile: {up.name}
OCR Used: {ocr_used}

InvoiceNumber: {inv_no}
InvoiceDate: {inv_date}

SellerName: {seller_name}
SellerSIRET: {seller_siret}
SellerVAT: {seller_vat}

BuyerName: {buyer_name}

TotalHT: {total_ht}
VATRatePercent: {vat_rate}

XML Validated: True
XML File: {xml_path}
PDF File: {pdf_path}
GeneratedAt: {datetime.now().isoformat()}
"""
                report_path.write_text(report_text, encoding="utf-8")

                # 7) Add to ZIP
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.xml", xml_bytes)
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.pdf", out_pdf_bytes)
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_report.txt", report_text)

                results.append(f"✅ {up.name} → OK ({inv_no})")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {up.name} → FAILED: {str(e)}")

        # Add a summary file into ZIP
        summary_text = "BULK SUMMARY\n-----------\n" + "\n".join(results) + "\n"
        zf.writestr("bulk_summary.txt", summary_text)

    progress.progress(100)
    status.write("✅ Bulk conversion finished.")

    st.subheader("Results")
    st.code("\n".join(results))

    st.info(f"📁 Saved batch folder locally: {batch_folder}")

    zip_buffer.seek(0)
    st.download_button(
        "Download ZIP (all PDFs + XML + reports)",
        data=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
        file_name=f"{batch_folder.name}.zip",
        mime="application/zip",
    )

def current_month_key() -> str:

def load_usage() -> dict:
    try:
        if USAGE_FILE.exists():
            return json.loads(USAGE_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception:
        pass
    return {}

def save_usage(data: dict):
    USAGE_FILE.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    USAGE_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

def get_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str) -> int:
    return int(data.get("months", {}).get(month_key, 0))

def increment_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str, n: int):
    if "months" not in data:
        data["months"] = {}
    data["months"][month_key] = get_month_count(data, month_key) + n

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path
import io
import os
import re
import zipfile
import json

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text


# -------------------------
# Free plan monthly limit
# -------------------------
FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH = 5
USAGE_FILE = Path("output") / "usage.json"

def current_month_key() -> str:
    return datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m")  # ex: "2025-12"

def load_usage() -> dict:
    try:
        if USAGE_FILE.exists():
            return json.loads(USAGE_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception:
        pass
    return {}

def save_usage(data: dict):
    USAGE_FILE.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    USAGE_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

def get_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str) -> int:
    return int(data.get("months", {}).get(month_key, 0))

def increment_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str, n: int):
    if "months" not in data:
        data["months"] = {}
    data["months"][month_key] = get_month_count(data, month_key) + n


# -------------------------
# Helpers
# -------------------------
def safe_name(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return "invoice"
    s = re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+", "_", s)
    return s[:80]

def to_decimal(s):
    if s is None:
        return None
    try:
        return Decimal(str(s).replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None

def compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht: Decimal, total_ttc: Decimal):
    if total_ht is None or total_ttc is None:
        return None
    if total_ht <= 0 or total_ttc < total_ht:
        return None
    vat_amount = total_ttc - total_ht
    rate = (vat_amount / total_ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    return rate


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }


# -------------------------
# UI
# -------------------------
st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Bulk Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Bulk Converter (Local Demo)")
st.caption("Bulk mode: upload many PDFs → download one ZIP with PDFs + XML + reports.")

use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (best results, may cost money later)", value=True)
azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False)

st.subheader("Seller (your company) — typed once for all PDFs")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", value="My Company")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", value="12345678900011")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", value="FR11123456789")

st.subheader("Defaults (used if OCR misses something)")
default_buyer_name = st.text_input("Default Buyer Name", value="Customer")
default_vat_rate = st.text_input("Default VAT rate % (used only if we cannot compute)", value="20")

uploaded_pdfs = st.file_uploader(
    "Upload invoice PDFs (you can select many)",
    type=["pdf"],
    accept_multiple_files=True
)

st.divider()

if not uploaded_pdfs:
    st.info("Upload PDFs to enable bulk conversion.")
    st.stop()

# ---- Free plan limit (monthly) ----
usage = load_usage()
month_key = current_month_key()
used_this_month = get_month_count(usage, month_key)

st.info(f"🧾 Free plan usage: {used_this_month}/{FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH} PDFs used this month ({month_key})")

remaining = FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH - used_this_month
if remaining <= 0:
    st.error("❌ Free limit reached for this month. (In real SaaS: ask user to upgrade.)")
    st.stop()

if len(uploaded_pdfs) > remaining:
    st.error(f"❌ You uploaded {len(uploaded_pdfs)} PDFs, but only {remaining} free PDFs remaining this month.")
    st.stop()

st.write(f"📄 PDFs selected: **{len(uploaded_pdfs)}**")

if st.button("Convert ALL to Factur-X (ZIP)"):
    out_root = Path("output")
    out_root.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    batch_folder = out_root / f"bulk_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
    batch_folder.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

    results = []
    zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()

    progress = st.progress(0)
    status = st.empty()

    default_vat_rate_dec = to_decimal(default_vat_rate)

    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
        for i, up in enumerate(uploaded_pdfs, start=1):
            status.write(f"⏳ Processing {i}/{len(uploaded_pdfs)}: **{up.name}**")
            progress.progress(int((i - 1) / len(uploaded_pdfs) * 100))

            try:
                pdf_bytes = up.read()

                # 1) Extract fields
                if use_azure:
                    if not azure_confirm:
                        raise Exception("Azure OCR is ON, but you did not confirm the cost checkbox.")
                    fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes)
                    ocr_used = "azure"
                else:
                    fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes)
                    ocr_used = "text"

                # 2) Build per-invoice values (with fallbacks)
                inv_no = fields.get("invoice_number") or Path(up.name).stem
                inv_no = safe_name(inv_no)

                inv_date = fields.get("invoice_date") or date.today()
                buyer_name = (fields.get("buyer_name") or default_buyer_name or "Customer").strip()

                total_ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                total_ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))

                vat_rate = None
                if total_ht is not None and total_ttc is not None:
                    vat_rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht, total_ttc)

                if vat_rate is None:
                    vat_rate = default_vat_rate_dec

                if total_ht is None:
                    raise Exception("Missing Total HT (SubTotal). OCR could not find it.")
                if vat_rate is None:
                    raise Exception("Missing VAT rate. OCR could not compute it and default VAT rate is invalid.")

                # 3) Build XML
                build_args = dict(
                    invoice_number=inv_no,
                    invoice_date=inv_date,
                    seller_name=seller_name,
                    seller_siret=seller_siret,
                    seller_vat=seller_vat,
                    buyer_name=buyer_name,
                    total_ht=total_ht,
                    vat_rate_percent=vat_rate,
                )

                xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(**build_args)

                # 4) Validate XML
                validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)

                # 5) Embed into PDF
                out_pdf_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

                # 6) Save locally
                xml_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml"
                pdf_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf"
                report_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_report.txt"

                xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
                pdf_path.write_bytes(out_pdf_bytes)

                report_text = f"""FACTUR-X BULK REPORT
-------------------
SourceFile: {up.name}
OCR Used: {ocr_used}

InvoiceNumber: {inv_no}
InvoiceDate: {inv_date}

SellerName: {seller_name}
SellerSIRET: {seller_siret}
SellerVAT: {seller_vat}

BuyerName: {buyer_name}

TotalHT: {total_ht}
VATRatePercent: {vat_rate}

XML Validated: True
XML File: {xml_path}
PDF File: {pdf_path}
GeneratedAt: {datetime.now().isoformat()}
"""
                report_path.write_text(report_text, encoding="utf-8")

                # 7) Add to ZIP
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.xml", xml_bytes)
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.pdf", out_pdf_bytes)
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_report.txt", report_text)

                results.append(f"✅ {up.name} → OK ({inv_no})")

                # ✅ Count only successful conversions
                increment_month_count(usage, month_key, 1)
                save_usage(usage)

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {up.name} → FAILED: {str(e)}")

        summary_text = "BULK SUMMARY\n-----------\n" + "\n".join(results) + "\n"
        zf.writestr("bulk_summary.txt", summary_text)

    progress.progress(100)
    status.write("✅ Bulk conversion finished.")

    st.subheader("Results")
    st.code("\n".join(results))

    st.info(f"📁 Saved batch folder locally: {batch_folder}")

    zip_buffer.seek(0)
    st.download_button(
        "Download ZIP (all PDFs + XML + reports)",
        data=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
        file_name=f"{batch_folder.name}.zip",
        mime="application/zip",
    )
