import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path
import io
import os
import re
import zipfile
import json

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text


# -------------------------
# Free plan monthly limit
# -------------------------
FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH = 5
USAGE_FILE = Path("output") / "usage.json"

def current_month_key() -> str:
    return datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m")  # ex: "2025-12"

def load_usage() -> dict:
    try:
        if USAGE_FILE.exists():
            return json.loads(USAGE_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception:
        pass
    return {}

def save_usage(data: dict):
    USAGE_FILE.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    USAGE_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

def get_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str) -> int:
    return int(data.get("months", {}).get(month_key, 0))

def increment_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str, n: int):
    if "months" not in data:
        data["months"] = {}
    data["months"][month_key] = get_month_count(data, month_key) + n


# -------------------------
# Helpers
# -------------------------
def safe_name(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return "invoice"
    s = re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+", "_", s)
    return s[:80]

def to_decimal(s):
    if s is None:
        return None
    try:
        return Decimal(str(s).replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None

def compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht: Decimal, total_ttc: Decimal):
    if total_ht is None or total_ttc is None:
        return None
    if total_ht <= 0 or total_ttc < total_ht:
        return None
    vat_amount = total_ttc - total_ht
    rate = (vat_amount / total_ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    return rate


def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }


# -------------------------
# UI
# -------------------------
st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Bulk Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Bulk Converter (Local Demo)")
st.caption("Bulk mode: upload many PDFs → download one ZIP with PDFs + XML + reports.")

use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (best results, may cost money later)", value=True)
azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False)

# ---- DEV reset (protected) ----
st.subheader("Developer tools (safe reset for testing)")
dev_code = st.text_input("Type DEV code to unlock reset", type="password", placeholder="(ask developer)")
if dev_code == "DEV123":
    if st.button("🔁 Reset free usage (DEV only)"):
        try:
            if USAGE_FILE.exists():
                USAGE_FILE.unlink()
            st.success("✅ Usage reset! Refresh the page.")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error(f"Could not reset usage: {e}")

st.divider()

st.subheader("Seller (your company) — typed once for all PDFs")
seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", value="My Company")
seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", value="12345678900011")
seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", value="FR11123456789")

st.subheader("Defaults (used if OCR misses something)")
default_buyer_name = st.text_input("Default Buyer Name", value="Customer")
default_vat_rate = st.text_input("Default VAT rate % (used only if we cannot compute)", value="20")

uploaded_pdfs = st.file_uploader(
    "Upload invoice PDFs (you can select many)",
    type=["pdf"],
    accept_multiple_files=True
)

st.divider()

if not uploaded_pdfs:
    st.info("Upload PDFs to enable bulk conversion.")
    st.stop()

# ---- Free plan limit (monthly) ----
usage = load_usage()
month_key = current_month_key()
used_this_month = get_month_count(usage, month_key)

st.info(f"🧾 Free plan usage: {used_this_month}/{FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH} PDFs used this month ({month_key})")

remaining = FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH - used_this_month
if remaining <= 0:
    st.error("❌ Free limit reached for this month. (In real SaaS: ask user to upgrade.)")
    st.stop()

if len(uploaded_pdfs) > remaining:
    st.error(f"❌ You uploaded {len(uploaded_pdfs)} PDFs, but only {remaining} free PDFs remaining this month.")
    st.stop()

st.write(f"📄 PDFs selected: **{len(uploaded_pdfs)}**")

if st.button("Convert ALL to Factur-X (ZIP)"):
    out_root = Path("output")
    out_root.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    batch_folder = out_root / f"bulk_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
    batch_folder.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

    results = []
    zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()

    progress = st.progress(0)
    status = st.empty()

    default_vat_rate_dec = to_decimal(default_vat_rate)

    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
        for i, up in enumerate(uploaded_pdfs, start=1):
            status.write(f"⏳ Processing {i}/{len(uploaded_pdfs)}: **{up.name}**")
            progress.progress(int((i - 1) / len(uploaded_pdfs) * 100))

            try:
                pdf_bytes = up.read()

                # 1) Extract fields
                if use_azure:
                    if not azure_confirm:
                        raise Exception("Azure OCR is ON, but you did not confirm the cost checkbox.")
                    fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes)
                    ocr_used = "azure"
                else:
                    fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes)
                    ocr_used = "text"

                # 2) Build per-invoice values (with fallbacks)
                inv_no = fields.get("invoice_number") or Path(up.name).stem
                inv_no = safe_name(inv_no)

                inv_date = fields.get("invoice_date") or date.today()
                buyer_name = (fields.get("buyer_name") or default_buyer_name or "Customer").strip()

                total_ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                total_ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))

                vat_rate = None
                if total_ht is not None and total_ttc is not None:
                    vat_rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht, total_ttc)

                if vat_rate is None:
                    vat_rate = default_vat_rate_dec

                if total_ht is None:
                    raise Exception("Missing Total HT (SubTotal). OCR could not find it.")
                if vat_rate is None:
                    raise Exception("Missing VAT rate. OCR could not compute it and default VAT rate is invalid.")

                # 3) Build XML
                build_args = dict(
                    invoice_number=inv_no,
                    invoice_date=inv_date,
                    seller_name=seller_name,
                    seller_siret=seller_siret,
                    seller_vat=seller_vat,
                    buyer_name=buyer_name,
                    total_ht=total_ht,
                    vat_rate_percent=vat_rate,
                )

                xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(**build_args)

                # 4) Validate XML
                validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)

                # 5) Embed into PDF
                out_pdf_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

                # 6) Save locally
                xml_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml"
                pdf_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf"
                report_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_report.txt"

                xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
                pdf_path.write_bytes(out_pdf_bytes)

                report_text = f"""FACTUR-X BULK REPORT
-------------------
SourceFile: {up.name}
OCR Used: {ocr_used}

InvoiceNumber: {inv_no}
InvoiceDate: {inv_date}

SellerName: {seller_name}
SellerSIRET: {seller_siret}
SellerVAT: {seller_vat}

BuyerName: {buyer_name}

TotalHT: {total_ht}
VATRatePercent: {vat_rate}

XML Validated: True
XML File: {xml_path}
PDF File: {pdf_path}
GeneratedAt: {datetime.now().isoformat()}
"""
                report_path.write_text(report_text, encoding="utf-8")

                # 7) Add to ZIP
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.xml", xml_bytes)
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.pdf", out_pdf_bytes)
                zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_report.txt", report_text)

                results.append(f"✅ {up.name} → OK ({inv_no})")

                # ✅ Count only successful conversions
                increment_month_count(usage, month_key, 1)
                save_usage(usage)

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {up.name} → FAILED: {str(e)}")

        summary_text = "BULK SUMMARY\n-----------\n" + "\n".join(results) + "\n"
        zf.writestr("bulk_summary.txt", summary_text)

    progress.progress(100)
    status.write("✅ Bulk conversion finished.")

    st.subheader("Results")
    st.code("\n".join(results))

    st.info(f"📁 Saved batch folder locally: {batch_folder}")

    zip_buffer.seek(0)
    st.download_button(
        "Download ZIP (all PDFs + XML + reports)",
        data=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
        file_name=f"{batch_folder.name}.zip",
        mime="application/zip",
    )

ChatGPT said:

Thought for 7s
Totally fair question — you’re noticing the real product difference. Think of it like this:

app.py = “One invoice, you can check everything carefully.”

bulk_app.py = “Many invoices, fast, with fewer questions asked.”

And for France: the government/PPF does NOT want you to upload 3 files.
They want one Factur-X PDF (a normal-looking PDF that secretly contains an XML inside it). That’s exactly what we generate.

The extra XML + report in bulk_app.py are just “debug / proof / audit” files for you, not for the government.

What does the real process look like for a customer / the French government?
What your customer sees
They receive a normal PDF invoice. It looks the same.

What the French portal/PPF “sees”
Inside that PDF, there’s a hidden file called factur-x.xml.
That hidden XML is what makes it “machine-readable” and compliant.

✅ So you still send/upload only ONE file: the Factur-X PDF.

Why does bulk_app.py download 3 things (ZIP with PDF + XML + report)?
Because in bulk, when something fails, you need to know why.

Factur-X PDF → the real deliverable (the only thing government needs)

XML (debug) → lets you inspect what was embedded

Report.txt → a simple receipt: what OCR extracted, totals, VAT rate, etc.

If you want, we can later add a switch like:
✅ “Include debug files (XML + report)” ON/OFF
So in “real mode” you only get PDFs.

Is “Auto-fill” missing in bulk_app.py?
Not really — it’s just done differently:

In app.py, auto-fill is a button that fills the form so you can edit it.

In bulk_app.py, auto-fill happens automatically per PDF during conversion using OCR + defaults (because showing 50 forms would be chaos).

So bulk is already doing “auto-fill”, just not showing it as a form-first step.

✅ Yes, we can add an “Auto-fill preview” button in bulk (example: show OCR results for the first PDF before converting all). That’s a common UX upgrade.

Comparison table: app.py vs bulk_app.py
Feature	app.py (Single)	bulk_app.py (Bulk)	Why it’s like that
Purpose	Convert 1 invoice	Convert many invoices	Different use cases
Auto-fill	Button fills form	OCR runs during conversion	Bulk can’t ask you to edit 50 invoices
Manual editing	Easy (you see all fields)	Not per-invoice (only defaults)	Bulk must be fast
Output	1 Factur-X PDF download	ZIP with PDFs + XML + reports	Bulk needs packaging + debugging
What gov needs	Factur-X PDF	Factur-X PDF	Always the same: one PDF with XML embedded
Debug visibility	Optional	Built-in	Bulk needs traceability
Best for	TPE who converts occasionally	PME who converts lots	Speed vs control
Why keep both? Why not only app.py?
Because they solve two different jobs:

If you want maximum correctness → use app.py (you can check, fix, re-download)

If you want maximum speed → use bulk_app.py (upload many → done)

Later, we can merge them into one app with two tabs:

Tab 1: Single converter

Tab 2: Bulk converter

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path
import io
import os
import re
import zipfile
import json

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text


# ============================================================
# Settings
# ============================================================
FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH = 5
USAGE_FILE = Path("output") / "usage.json"
DEV_RESET_CODE = "DEV310899"  # ✅ your DEV code


# ============================================================
# Small helpers
# ============================================================
def safe_name(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return "invoice"
    s = re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+", "_", s)
    return s[:80]


def to_decimal(s):
    if s is None:
        return None
    try:
        return Decimal(str(s).replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None


def compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht: Decimal, total_ttc: Decimal):
    if total_ht is None or total_ttc is None:
        return None
    if total_ht <= 0 or total_ttc < total_ht:
        return None
    vat_amount = total_ttc - total_ht
    rate = (vat_amount / total_ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    return rate


def current_month_key() -> str:
    return datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m")


def load_usage() -> dict:
    try:
        if USAGE_FILE.exists():
            return json.loads(USAGE_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception:
        pass
    return {}


def save_usage(data: dict):
    USAGE_FILE.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    USAGE_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")


def get_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str) -> int:
    return int(data.get("months", {}).get(month_key, 0))


def increment_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str, n: int):
    if "months" not in data:
        data["months"] = {}
    data["months"][month_key] = get_month_count(data, month_key) + n


# ============================================================
# Azure OCR
# ============================================================
def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }


# ============================================================
# UI: SINGLE CONVERTER
# ============================================================
def render_single():
    st.subheader("Single converter (1 PDF → 1 Factur-X PDF)")

    use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (may cost money later)", value=True, key="single_use_azure")
    azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False, key="single_azure_confirm")

    uploaded_pdf = st.file_uploader("Upload your invoice PDF", type=["pdf"], key="single_pdf")

    colA, colB = st.columns(2)

    if uploaded_pdf:
        pdf_bytes_now = uploaded_pdf.read()

        with colA:
            if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)", key="single_btn_text"):
                try:
                    fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_now)
                    st.session_state["single_invoice_number"] = fields.get("invoice_number") or st.session_state.get("single_invoice_number", "INV-001")
                    st.session_state["single_buyer_name"] = fields.get("buyer_name") or st.session_state.get("single_buyer_name", "Customer Name")
                    st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Check fields below.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Text auto-fill failed: {e}")

        with colB:
            if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)", key="single_btn_azure"):
                try:
                    if not use_azure:
                        st.warning("Turn ON Azure OCR checkbox first.")
                    elif not azure_confirm:
                        st.warning("Tick the cost confirmation checkbox first.")
                    else:
                        fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_now)
                        if fields.get("invoice_number"):
                            st.session_state["single_invoice_number"] = safe_name(fields["invoice_number"])
                        if fields.get("invoice_date"):
                            st.session_state["single_invoice_date"] = fields["invoice_date"]
                        if fields.get("buyer_name"):
                            st.session_state["single_buyer_name"] = fields["buyer_name"]
                        if fields.get("seller_name"):
                            st.session_state["single_seller_name"] = fields["seller_name"]
                        if fields.get("total_ht_str"):
                            st.session_state["single_total_ht"] = str(fields["total_ht_str"])
                        # Optional: if we can compute VAT rate
                        ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                        ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))
                        rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(ht, ttc) if ht and ttc else None
                        if rate is not None:
                            st.session_state["single_vat_rate"] = str(rate)
                        st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Check fields below.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Azure auto-fill failed: {e}")

        # IMPORTANT: put bytes back for later use
        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)

    st.divider()
    st.markdown("### Invoice details")

    invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number",
                                   value=st.session_state.get("single_invoice_number", "INV-001"),
                                   key="single_invoice_number")

    invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_invoice_date", date.today()),
                                 key="single_invoice_date")

    st.markdown("### Seller (your company)")
    seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name",
                                value=st.session_state.get("single_seller_name", "My Company"),
                                key="single_seller_name")
    seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_seller_siret", "12345678900011"),
                                 key="single_seller_siret")
    seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)",
                               value=st.session_state.get("single_seller_vat", "FR11123456789"),
                               key="single_seller_vat")

    st.markdown("### Buyer (your customer)")
    buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name",
                               value=st.session_state.get("single_buyer_name", "Customer Name"),
                               key="single_buyer_name")

    st.markdown("### Amounts")
    total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_total_ht", "100.00"),
                                 key="single_total_ht")
    vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_vat_rate", "20"),
                                 key="single_vat_rate")

    # Show a little helper line (kid-friendly)
    try:
        ht = Decimal(total_ht_str.replace(",", "."))
        vr = Decimal(vat_rate_str.replace(",", "."))
        vat_amount = (ht * vr / Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
        ttc = (ht + vat_amount).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
        st.caption(f"🧮 VAT amount: {vat_amount} | Total TTC: {ttc}")
    except Exception:
        pass

    if not uploaded_pdf:
        st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")
        return

    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF", key="single_generate"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(total_ht_str.replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(vat_rate_str.replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        # Validate XML (trust layer)
        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        # Re-read PDF bytes (important)
        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        # Save locally (dev convenience)
        out_dir = Path("output")
        out_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        out_pdf_path = out_dir / f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.pdf"
        out_xml_path = out_dir / f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.xml"
        out_pdf_path.write_bytes(out_bytes)
        out_xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
        st.info(f"📁 Saved locally: {out_pdf_path}")

        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
            key="single_dl_pdf"
        )

        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
            st=False if False else None,
            key="single_dl_xml"
        )


# ============================================================
# UI: BULK CONVERTER
# ============================================================
def render_bulk():
    st.subheader("Bulk converter (many PDFs → one ZIP)")

    use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (best results, may cost money later)", value=True, key="bulk_use_azure")
    azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False, key="bulk_azure_confirm")

    st.markdown("### Developer tools (DEV only)")
    dev_code = st.text_input("Type DEV code to unlock DEV tools", type="password", key="bulk_dev_code")
    dev_unlocked = (dev_code == DEV_RESET_CODE)

    pro_mode = False
    if dev_unlocked:
        pro_mode = st.checkbox("⭐ PRO mode (unlimited conversions)", value=False, key="bulk_pro_mode")
        col1, col2 = st.columns(2)
        with col1:
            if st.button("🔁 Reset free usage (DEV only)", key="bulk_reset_usage"):
                try:
                    if USAGE_FILE.exists():
                        USAGE_FILE.unlink()
                    st.success("✅ Usage reset! Refresh the page.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Could not reset usage: {e}")
        with col2:
            st.success("✅ DEV tools unlocked")
    else:
        st.info("DEV tools locked (enter code to unlock).")

    st.divider()

    st.markdown("### Seller (your company) — typed once for all PDFs")
    seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", value="My Company", key="bulk_seller_name")
    seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", value="12345678900011", key="bulk_seller_siret")
    seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", value="FR11123456789", key="bulk_seller_vat")

    st.markdown("### Defaults (used if OCR misses something)")
    default_buyer_name = st.text_input("Default Buyer Name", value="Customer", key="bulk_default_buyer")
    default_vat_rate = st.text_input("Default VAT rate % (used only if we cannot compute)", value="20", key="bulk_default_vat")

    uploaded_pdfs = st.file_uploader(
        "Upload invoice PDFs (you can select many)",
        type=["pdf"],
        accept_multiple_files=True,
        key="bulk_pdfs"
    )

    if not uploaded_pdfs:
        st.info("Upload PDFs to enable bulk conversion.")
        return

    # Free plan limit (monthly)
    usage = load_usage()
    month_key = current_month_key()
    used_this_month = get_month_count(usage, month_key)

    if pro_mode:
        st.success("⭐ PRO mode is ON → Unlimited conversions.")
    else:
        st.info(f"🧾 Free plan usage: {used_this_month}/{FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH} PDFs used this month ({month_key})")
        remaining = FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH - used_this_month
        if remaining <= 0:
            st.error("❌ Free limit reached for this month. (In real SaaS: ask user to upgrade.)")
            return
        if len(uploaded_pdfs) > remaining:
            st.error(f"❌ You uploaded {len(uploaded_pdfs)} PDFs, but only {remaining} free PDFs remaining this month.")
            return

    st.write(f"📄 PDFs selected: **{len(uploaded_pdfs)}**")

    if st.button("Convert ALL to Factur-X (ZIP)", key="bulk_convert_btn"):
        out_root = Path("output")
        out_root.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        batch_folder = out_root / f"bulk_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
        batch_folder.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        results = []
        zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()

        progress = st.progress(0)
        status = st.empty()

        default_vat_rate_dec = to_decimal(default_vat_rate)

        with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
            for i, up in enumerate(uploaded_pdfs, start=1):
                status.write(f"⏳ Processing {i}/{len(uploaded_pdfs)}: **{up.name}**")
                progress.progress(int((i - 1) / len(uploaded_pdfs) * 100))

                try:
                    pdf_bytes = up.read()

                    # 1) Extract fields
                    if use_azure:
                        if not azure_confirm:
                            raise Exception("Azure OCR is ON, but you did not confirm the cost checkbox.")
                        fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes)
                        ocr_used = "azure"
                    else:
                        fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes)
                        ocr_used = "text"

                    # 2) Build per-invoice values (with fallbacks)
                    inv_no = fields.get("invoice_number") or Path(up.name).stem
                    inv_no = safe_name(inv_no)

                    inv_date = fields.get("invoice_date") or date.today()
                    buyer_name = (fields.get("buyer_name") or default_buyer_name or "Customer").strip()

                    total_ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                    total_ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))

                    vat_rate = None
                    if total_ht is not None and total_ttc is not None:
                        vat_rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht, total_ttc)

                    if vat_rate is None:
                        vat_rate = default_vat_rate_dec

                    if total_ht is None:
                        raise Exception("Missing Total HT (SubTotal). OCR could not find it.")
                    if vat_rate is None:
                        raise Exception("Missing VAT rate. OCR could not compute it and default VAT rate is invalid.")

                    # 3) Build XML
                    xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
                        invoice_number=inv_no,
                        invoice_date=inv_date,
                        seller_name=seller_name,
                        seller_siret=seller_siret,
                        seller_vat=seller_vat,
                        buyer_name=buyer_name,
                        total_ht=total_ht,
                        vat_rate_percent=vat_rate,
                    )

                    # 4) Validate XML
                    validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)

                    # 5) Embed into PDF
                    out_pdf_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

                    # 6) Save locally
                    xml_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml"
                    pdf_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf"
                    report_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_report.txt"

                    xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
                    pdf_path.write_bytes(out_pdf_bytes)

                    report_text = f"""FACTUR-X BULK REPORT
-------------------
SourceFile: {up.name}
OCR Used: {ocr_used}

InvoiceNumber: {inv_no}
InvoiceDate: {inv_date}

SellerName: {seller_name}
SellerSIRET: {seller_siret}
SellerVAT: {seller_vat}

BuyerName: {buyer_name}

TotalHT: {total_ht}
VATRatePercent: {vat_rate}

XML Validated: True
XML File: {xml_path}
PDF File: {pdf_path}
GeneratedAt: {datetime.now().isoformat()}
"""
                    report_path.write_text(report_text, encoding="utf-8")

                    # 7) Add to ZIP
                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.xml", xml_bytes)
                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.pdf", out_pdf_bytes)
                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_report.txt", report_text)

                    results.append(f"✅ {up.name} → OK ({inv_no})")

                    # Count only successful conversions (FREE mode only)
                    if not pro_mode:
                        usage = load_usage()
                        increment_month_count(usage, month_key, 1)
                        save_usage(usage)

                except Exception as e:
                    results.append(f"❌ {up.name} → FAILED: {str(e)}")

            summary_text = "BULK SUMMARY\n-----------\n" + "\n".join(results) + "\n"
            zf.writestr("bulk_summary.txt", summary_text)

        progress.progress(100)
        status.write("✅ Bulk conversion finished.")

        st.subheader("Results")
        st.code("\n".join(results))
        st.info(f"📁 Saved batch folder locally: {batch_folder}")

        zip_buffer.seek(0)
        st.download_button(
            "Download ZIP (all PDFs + XML + reports)",
            data=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
            file_name=f"{batch_folder.name}.zip",
            mime="application/zip",
            key="bulk_dl_zip"
        )


# ============================================================

st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Converter (Local Demo)")

import streamlit as st
from datetime import date, datetime
from decimal import Decimal, InvalidOperation, ROUND_HALF_UP
from pathlib import Path
import io
import os
import re
import zipfile
import json

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from azure.core.credentials import AzureKeyCredential
from azure.ai.documentintelligence import DocumentIntelligenceClient

from facturx_engine import embed_facturx
from facturx_xml import build_facturx_minimum_xml
from validator import validate_facturx_minimum

from pdf_autofill import extract_fields as extract_fields_text


# ============================================================
# Settings
# ============================================================
FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH = 5
USAGE_FILE = Path("output") / "usage.json"
DEV_RESET_CODE = "DEV310899"  # ✅ your DEV code


# ============================================================
# Small helpers
# ============================================================
def safe_name(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return "invoice"
    s = re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+", "_", s)
    return s[:80]


def to_decimal(s):
    if s is None:
        return None
    try:
        return Decimal(str(s).replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None


def compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht: Decimal, total_ttc: Decimal):
    if total_ht is None or total_ttc is None:
        return None
    if total_ht <= 0 or total_ttc < total_ht:
        return None
    vat_amount = total_ttc - total_ht
    rate = (vat_amount / total_ht * Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
    return rate


def current_month_key() -> str:
    return datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m")


def load_usage() -> dict:
    try:
        if USAGE_FILE.exists():
            return json.loads(USAGE_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    except Exception:
        pass
    return {}


def save_usage(data: dict):
    USAGE_FILE.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    USAGE_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")


def get_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str) -> int:
    return int(data.get("months", {}).get(month_key, 0))


def increment_month_count(data: dict, month_key: str, n: int):
    if "months" not in data:
        data["months"] = {}
    data["months"][month_key] = get_month_count(data, month_key) + n


# ============================================================
# Azure OCR
# ============================================================
def azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes: bytes) -> dict:
    load_dotenv()
    endpoint = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT")
    key = os.getenv("DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY")

    if not endpoint or not key:
        raise RuntimeError("Missing DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_ENDPOINT or DOCUMENTINTELLIGENCE_API_KEY in .env")

    client = DocumentIntelligenceClient(endpoint=endpoint, credential=AzureKeyCredential(key))

    poller = client.begin_analyze_document(
        model_id="prebuilt-invoice",
        body=io.BytesIO(pdf_bytes),
    )
    result = poller.result()

    if not result.documents:
        return {}

    doc = result.documents[0]
    fields = doc.fields or {}

    def content(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            return f.get("content")
        except Exception:
            return None

    def number(name: str):
        f = fields.get(name)
        if not f:
            return None
        try:
            vc = f.get("valueCurrency")
            if isinstance(vc, dict) and "amount" in vc:
                return str(vc["amount"])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return content(name)

    inv_date_raw = content("InvoiceDate")
    inv_date = None
    if inv_date_raw:
        try:
            inv_date = datetime.strptime(inv_date_raw.strip(), "%Y-%m-%d").date()
        except Exception:
            inv_date = None

    return {
        "invoice_number": content("InvoiceId") or content("InvoiceNumber"),
        "invoice_date": inv_date,
        "buyer_name": content("CustomerName"),
        "seller_name": content("VendorName"),
        "total_ht_str": number("SubTotal"),
        "total_ttc_str": number("InvoiceTotal"),
    }


# ============================================================
# UI: SINGLE CONVERTER
# ============================================================
def render_single():
    st.subheader("Single converter (1 PDF → 1 Factur-X PDF)")

    use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (may cost money later)", value=True, key="single_use_azure")
    azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False, key="single_azure_confirm")

    uploaded_pdf = st.file_uploader("Upload your invoice PDF", type=["pdf"], key="single_pdf")

    colA, colB = st.columns(2)

    if uploaded_pdf:
        pdf_bytes_now = uploaded_pdf.read()

        with colA:
            if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (text)", key="single_btn_text"):
                try:
                    fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes_now)
                    st.session_state["single_invoice_number"] = fields.get("invoice_number") or st.session_state.get("single_invoice_number", "INV-001")
                    st.session_state["single_buyer_name"] = fields.get("buyer_name") or st.session_state.get("single_buyer_name", "Customer Name")
                    st.success("✅ Auto-fill (text) done. Check fields below.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Text auto-fill failed: {e}")

        with colB:
            if st.button("Auto-fill from PDF (Azure OCR)", key="single_btn_azure"):
                try:
                    if not use_azure:
                        st.warning("Turn ON Azure OCR checkbox first.")
                    elif not azure_confirm:
                        st.warning("Tick the cost confirmation checkbox first.")
                    else:
                        fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes_now)
                        if fields.get("invoice_number"):
                            st.session_state["single_invoice_number"] = safe_name(fields["invoice_number"])
                        if fields.get("invoice_date"):
                            st.session_state["single_invoice_date"] = fields["invoice_date"]
                        if fields.get("buyer_name"):
                            st.session_state["single_buyer_name"] = fields["buyer_name"]
                        if fields.get("seller_name"):
                            st.session_state["single_seller_name"] = fields["seller_name"]
                        if fields.get("total_ht_str"):
                            st.session_state["single_total_ht"] = str(fields["total_ht_str"])

                        ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                        ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))
                        rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(ht, ttc) if ht and ttc else None
                        if rate is not None:
                            st.session_state["single_vat_rate"] = str(rate)

                        st.success("✅ Auto-fill (Azure OCR) done. Check fields below.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Azure auto-fill failed: {e}")

        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)

    st.divider()
    st.markdown("### Invoice details")

    invoice_number = st.text_input("Invoice Number",
                                   value=st.session_state.get("single_invoice_number", "INV-001"),
                                   key="single_invoice_number")

    invoice_date = st.date_input("Invoice Date",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_invoice_date", date.today()),
                                 key="single_invoice_date")

    st.markdown("### Seller (your company)")
    seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name",
                                value=st.session_state.get("single_seller_name", "My Company"),
                                key="single_seller_name")
    seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_seller_siret", "12345678900011"),
                                 key="single_seller_siret")
    seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)",
                               value=st.session_state.get("single_seller_vat", "FR11123456789"),
                               key="single_seller_vat")

    st.markdown("### Buyer (your customer)")
    buyer_name = st.text_input("Buyer Name",
                               value=st.session_state.get("single_buyer_name", "Customer Name"),
                               key="single_buyer_name")

    st.markdown("### Amounts")
    total_ht_str = st.text_input("Total HT (ex: 100.00)",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_total_ht", "100.00"),
                                 key="single_total_ht")
    vat_rate_str = st.text_input("VAT rate % (ex: 20)",
                                 value=st.session_state.get("single_vat_rate", "20"),
                                 key="single_vat_rate")

    try:
        ht = Decimal(total_ht_str.replace(",", "."))
        vr = Decimal(vat_rate_str.replace(",", "."))
        vat_amount = (ht * vr / Decimal("100")).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
        ttc = (ht + vat_amount).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
        st.caption(f"🧮 VAT amount: {vat_amount} | Total TTC: {ttc}")
    except Exception:
        pass

    if not uploaded_pdf:
        st.info("Upload a PDF to enable generation.")
        return

    if st.button("Generate Factur-X PDF", key="single_generate"):
        try:
            total_ht = Decimal(total_ht_str.replace(",", "."))
            vat_rate_percent = Decimal(vat_rate_str.replace(",", "."))
        except InvalidOperation:
            st.error("Amounts not valid. Use numbers like 100.00 and 20")
            st.stop()

        xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
            invoice_number=invoice_number,
            invoice_date=invoice_date,
            seller_name=seller_name,
            seller_siret=seller_siret,
            seller_vat=seller_vat,
            buyer_name=buyer_name,
            total_ht=total_ht,
            vat_rate_percent=vat_rate_percent,
        )

        try:
            validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)
            st.success("✅ XML validated (Factur-X MINIMUM)")
        except Exception as e:
            st.error("❌ XML is NOT valid. Fix fields before generating.")
            st.code(str(e))
            st.stop()

        uploaded_pdf.seek(0)
        pdf_bytes = uploaded_pdf.read()

        out_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

        out_dir = Path("output")
        out_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        out_pdf_path = out_dir / f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.pdf"
        out_xml_path = out_dir / f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.xml"
        out_pdf_path.write_bytes(out_bytes)
        out_xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
        st.info(f"📁 Saved locally: {out_pdf_path}")

        st.download_button(
            "Download Factur-X PDF",
            data=out_bytes,
            file_name=f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.pdf",
            mime="application/pdf",
            key="single_dl_pdf"
        )

        st.download_button(
            "Download XML (debug)",
            data=xml_bytes,
            file_name=f"{safe_name(invoice_number)}_facturx.xml",
            mime="application/xml",
            key="single_dl_xml"
        )


# ============================================================
# UI: BULK CONVERTER
# ============================================================
def render_bulk():
    st.subheader("Bulk converter (many PDFs → one ZIP)")

    use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (best results, may cost money later)", value=True, key="bulk_use_azure")
    azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False, key="bulk_azure_confirm")

    st.markdown("### Developer tools (DEV only)")
    dev_code = st.text_input("Type DEV code to unlock DEV tools", type="password", key="bulk_dev_code")
    dev_unlocked = (dev_code == DEV_RESET_CODE)

    pro_mode = False
    if dev_unlocked:
        pro_mode = st.checkbox("⭐ PRO mode (unlimited conversions)", value=False, key="bulk_pro_mode")
        col1, col2 = st.columns(2)
        with col1:
            if st.button("🔁 Reset free usage (DEV only)", key="bulk_reset_usage"):
                try:
                    if USAGE_FILE.exists():
                        USAGE_FILE.unlink()
                    st.success("✅ Usage reset! Refresh the page.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Could not reset usage: {e}")
        with col2:
            st.success("✅ DEV tools unlocked")
    else:
        st.info("DEV tools locked (enter code to unlock).")

    st.divider()

    st.markdown("### Seller (your company) — typed once for all PDFs")
    seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", value="My Company", key="bulk_seller_name")
    seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", value="12345678900011", key="bulk_seller_siret")
    seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", value="FR11123456789", key="bulk_seller_vat")

    st.markdown("### Defaults (used if OCR misses something)")
    default_buyer_name = st.text_input("Default Buyer Name", value="Customer", key="bulk_default_buyer")
    default_vat_rate = st.text_input("Default VAT rate % (used only if we cannot compute)", value="20", key="bulk_default_vat")

    uploaded_pdfs = st.file_uploader(
        "Upload invoice PDFs (you can select many)",
        type=["pdf"],
        accept_multiple_files=True,
        key="bulk_pdfs"
    )

    if not uploaded_pdfs:
        st.info("Upload PDFs to enable bulk conversion.")
        return

    usage = load_usage()
    month_key = current_month_key()
    used_this_month = get_month_count(usage, month_key)

    if pro_mode:
        st.success("⭐ PRO mode is ON → Unlimited conversions.")
    else:
        st.info(f"🧾 Free plan usage: {used_this_month}/{FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH} PDFs used this month ({month_key})")
        remaining = FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH - used_this_month
        if remaining <= 0:
            st.error("❌ Free limit reached for this month. (In real SaaS: ask user to upgrade.)")
            return
        if len(uploaded_pdfs) > remaining:
            st.error(f"❌ You uploaded {len(uploaded_pdfs)} PDFs, but only {remaining} free PDFs remaining this month.")
            return

    st.write(f"📄 PDFs selected: **{len(uploaded_pdfs)}**")

    if st.button("Convert ALL to Factur-X (ZIP)", key="bulk_convert_btn"):
        out_root = Path("output")
        out_root.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        batch_folder = out_root / f"bulk_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
        batch_folder.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        results = []
        zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()

        progress = st.progress(0)
        status = st.empty()

        default_vat_rate_dec = to_decimal(default_vat_rate)

        with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
            for i, up in enumerate(uploaded_pdfs, start=1):
                status.write(f"⏳ Processing {i}/{len(uploaded_pdfs)}: **{up.name}**")
                progress.progress(int((i - 1) / len(uploaded_pdfs) * 100))

                try:
                    pdf_bytes = up.read()

                    if use_azure:
                        if not azure_confirm:
                            raise Exception("Azure OCR is ON, but you did not confirm the cost checkbox.")
                        fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes)
                    else:
                        fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes)

                    inv_no = fields.get("invoice_number") or Path(up.name).stem
                    inv_no = safe_name(inv_no)

                    inv_date = fields.get("invoice_date") or date.today()
                    buyer_name = (fields.get("buyer_name") or default_buyer_name or "Customer").strip()

                    total_ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                    total_ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))

                    vat_rate = None
                    if total_ht is not None and total_ttc is not None:
                        vat_rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht, total_ttc)

                    if vat_rate is None:
                        vat_rate = default_vat_rate_dec

                    if total_ht is None:
                        raise Exception("Missing Total HT (SubTotal). OCR could not find it.")
                    if vat_rate is None:
                        raise Exception("Missing VAT rate. OCR could not compute it and default VAT rate is invalid.")

                    xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
                        invoice_number=inv_no,
                        invoice_date=inv_date,
                        seller_name=seller_name,
                        seller_siret=seller_siret,
                        seller_vat=seller_vat,
                        buyer_name=buyer_name,
                        total_ht=total_ht,
                        vat_rate_percent=vat_rate,
                    )

                    validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)

                    out_pdf_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

                    xml_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml"
                    pdf_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf"
                    report_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_report.txt"

                    xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)
                    pdf_path.write_bytes(out_pdf_bytes)

                    report_text = f"""FACTUR-X BULK REPORT
-------------------
SourceFile: {up.name}

InvoiceNumber: {inv_no}
InvoiceDate: {inv_date}

SellerName: {seller_name}
SellerSIRET: {seller_siret}
SellerVAT: {seller_vat}

BuyerName: {buyer_name}

TotalHT: {total_ht}
VATRatePercent: {vat_rate}

XML Validated: True
GeneratedAt: {datetime.now().isoformat()}
"""
                    report_path.write_text(report_text, encoding="utf-8")

                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.xml", xml_bytes)
                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_facturx.pdf", out_pdf_bytes)
                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}/{inv_no}_report.txt", report_text)

                    results.append(f"✅ {up.name} → OK ({inv_no})")

                    if not pro_mode:
                        usage = load_usage()
                        increment_month_count(usage, month_key, 1)
                        save_usage(usage)

                except Exception as e:
                    results.append(f"❌ {up.name} → FAILED: {str(e)}")

            summary_text = "BULK SUMMARY\n-----------\n" + "\n".join(results) + "\n"
            zf.writestr("bulk_summary.txt", summary_text)

        progress.progress(100)
        status.write("✅ Bulk conversion finished.")

        st.subheader("Results")
        st.code("\n".join(results))
        st.info(f"📁 Saved batch folder locally: {batch_folder}")

        zip_buffer.seek(0)
        st.download_button(
            "Download ZIP (all PDFs + XML + reports)",
            data=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
            file_name=f"{batch_folder.name}.zip",
            mime="application/zip",
            key="bulk_dl_zip"
        )


# ============================================================
# Main App (Tabs)
# ============================================================
st.set_page_config(page_title="Factur-X Converter", layout="centered")
st.title("Factur-X Converter (Local Demo)")
st.caption("DEV build: Single + Bulk in one app. Later we hide debug buttons in production.")

tab1, tab2 = st.tabs(["Single converter", "Bulk converter"])

with tab1:
    render_single()

with tab2:
    render_bulk()

def render_bulk():
    st.subheader("Bulk converter (many PDFs → one ZIP of PDFs only)")

    use_azure = st.checkbox("Use Azure OCR (best results, may cost money later)", value=True, key="bulk_use_azure")
    azure_confirm = st.checkbox("I understand Azure OCR may cost money", value=False, key="bulk_azure_confirm")

    # ✅ Production-style: ZIP only contains PDFs
    include_debug = st.checkbox("DEV only: Also include XML + report in ZIP", value=False, key="bulk_include_debug")

    st.markdown("### Developer tools (DEV only)")
    dev_code = st.text_input("Type DEV code to unlock DEV tools", type="password", key="bulk_dev_code")
    dev_unlocked = (dev_code == DEV_RESET_CODE)

    pro_mode = False
    if dev_unlocked:
        pro_mode = st.checkbox("⭐ PRO mode (unlimited conversions)", value=False, key="bulk_pro_mode")
        col1, col2 = st.columns(2)
        with col1:
            if st.button("🔁 Reset free usage (DEV only)", key="bulk_reset_usage"):
                try:
                    if USAGE_FILE.exists():
                        USAGE_FILE.unlink()
                    st.success("✅ Usage reset! Refresh the page.")
                except Exception as e:
                    st.error(f"Could not reset usage: {e}")
        with col2:
            st.success("✅ DEV tools unlocked")
    else:
        st.info("DEV tools locked (enter code to unlock).")

    st.divider()

    st.markdown("### Seller (your company) — typed once for all PDFs")
    seller_name = st.text_input("Seller Name", value="My Company", key="bulk_seller_name")
    seller_siret = st.text_input("Seller SIRET", value="12345678900011", key="bulk_seller_siret")
    seller_vat = st.text_input("Seller VAT (FR...)", value="FR11123456789", key="bulk_seller_vat")

    st.markdown("### Defaults (used if OCR misses something)")
    default_buyer_name = st.text_input("Default Buyer Name", value="Customer", key="bulk_default_buyer")
    default_vat_rate = st.text_input("Default VAT rate % (used only if we cannot compute)", value="20", key="bulk_default_vat")

    uploaded_pdfs = st.file_uploader(
        "Upload invoice PDFs (you can select many)",
        type=["pdf"],
        accept_multiple_files=True,
        key="bulk_pdfs"
    )

    if not uploaded_pdfs:
        st.info("Upload PDFs to enable bulk conversion.")
        return

    usage = load_usage()
    month_key = current_month_key()
    used_this_month = get_month_count(usage, month_key)

    if pro_mode:
        st.success("⭐ PRO mode is ON → Unlimited conversions.")
    else:
        st.info(f"🧾 Free plan usage: {used_this_month}/{FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH} PDFs used this month ({month_key})")
        remaining = FREE_LIMIT_PER_MONTH - used_this_month
        if remaining <= 0:
            st.error("❌ Free limit reached for this month. (In real SaaS: ask user to upgrade.)")
            return
        if len(uploaded_pdfs) > remaining:
            st.error(f"❌ You uploaded {len(uploaded_pdfs)} PDFs, but only {remaining} free PDFs remaining this month.")
            return

    st.write(f"📄 PDFs selected: **{len(uploaded_pdfs)}**")

    if st.button("Convert ALL to Factur-X (ZIP)", key="bulk_convert_btn"):
        out_root = Path("output")
        out_root.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        batch_folder = out_root / f"bulk_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
        batch_folder.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        results = []
        zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()

        progress = st.progress(0)
        status = st.empty()

        default_vat_rate_dec = to_decimal(default_vat_rate)

        with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
            for i, up in enumerate(uploaded_pdfs, start=1):
                status.write(f"⏳ Processing {i}/{len(uploaded_pdfs)}: **{up.name}**")
                progress.progress(int((i - 1) / len(uploaded_pdfs) * 100))

                try:
                    pdf_bytes = up.read()

                    if use_azure:
                        if not azure_confirm:
                            raise Exception("Azure OCR is ON, but you did not confirm the cost checkbox.")
                        fields = azure_extract_invoice_fields(pdf_bytes)
                    else:
                        fields = extract_fields_text(pdf_bytes)

                    inv_no = fields.get("invoice_number") or Path(up.name).stem
                    inv_no = safe_name(inv_no)

                    inv_date = fields.get("invoice_date") or date.today()
                    buyer_name = (fields.get("buyer_name") or default_buyer_name or "Customer").strip()

                    total_ht = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ht_str"))
                    total_ttc = to_decimal(fields.get("total_ttc_str"))

                    vat_rate = None
                    if total_ht is not None and total_ttc is not None:
                        vat_rate = compute_vat_rate_percent(total_ht, total_ttc)

                    if vat_rate is None:
                        vat_rate = default_vat_rate_dec

                    if total_ht is None:
                        raise Exception("Missing Total HT (SubTotal). OCR could not find it.")
                    if vat_rate is None:
                        raise Exception("Missing VAT rate. OCR could not compute it and default VAT rate is invalid.")

                    xml_bytes = build_facturx_minimum_xml(
                        invoice_number=inv_no,
                        invoice_date=inv_date,
                        seller_name=seller_name,
                        seller_siret=seller_siret,
                        seller_vat=seller_vat,
                        buyer_name=buyer_name,
                        total_ht=total_ht,
                        vat_rate_percent=vat_rate,
                    )

                    validate_facturx_minimum(xml_bytes)

                    out_pdf_bytes = embed_facturx(pdf_bytes, xml_bytes)

                    # ✅ Save locally: ALWAYS PDF
                    pdf_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf"
                    pdf_path.write_bytes(out_pdf_bytes)

                    # ✅ ZIP: ALWAYS only PDFs (clean for customers / govt)
                    zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}_facturx.pdf", out_pdf_bytes)

                    # ✅ Optional DEV debug (XML + report)
                    if include_debug:
                        xml_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml"
                        report_path = batch_folder / f"{inv_no}_report.txt"

                        xml_path.write_bytes(xml_bytes)

                        report_text = f"""FACTUR-X BULK REPORT
-------------------
SourceFile: {up.name}

InvoiceNumber: {inv_no}
InvoiceDate: {inv_date}

SellerName: {seller_name}
SellerSIRET: {seller_siret}
SellerVAT: {seller_vat}

BuyerName: {buyer_name}

TotalHT: {total_ht}
VATRatePercent: {vat_rate}

XML Validated: True
GeneratedAt: {datetime.now().isoformat()}
"""
                        report_path.write_text(report_text, encoding="utf-8")

                        zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}_facturx.xml", xml_bytes)
                        zf.writestr(f"{inv_no}_report.txt", report_text)

                    results.append(f"✅ {up.name} → OK ({inv_no})")

                    if not pro_mode:
                        usage = load_usage()
                        increment_month_count(usage, month_key, 1)
                        save_usage(usage)

                except Exception as e:
                    results.append(f"❌ {up.name} → FAILED: {str(e)}")

        progress.progress(100)
        status.write("✅ Bulk conversion finished.")

        st.subheader("Results")
        st.code("\n".join(results))
        st.info(f"📁 Saved batch folder locally: {batch_folder}")

        zip_buffer.seek(0)
        st.download_button(
            "Download ZIP (PDFs only)",
            data=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
            file_name=f"{batch_folder.name}.zip",
            mime="application/zip",
            key="bulk_dl_zip"
        )
